Actor SkillCountSetter : CustomInventory
{
	var int user_skill;
	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	Inventory.MaxAmount 0
	States
	{
	Pickup:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SkillCount",5,"Set5",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SkillCount",4,"Set4",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SkillCount",3,"Set3",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SkillCount",2,"Set2",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SkillCount",1,"Set1",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		Stop
	Set5:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_skill",5)
		Stop
	Set4:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_skill",4)
		Stop
	Set3:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_skill",3)
		Stop
	Set2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_skill",2)
		Stop
	Set1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_skill",1)
		Stop
	}
}

Actor L4DTank //cyberdemon
{
	var int user_skill;
	DropItem DMSoulFragment
	Monster	+DONTCORPSE RipLevelMin 1
	+BOSS
	+BOSSDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOICEDEATH
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+DONTBLAST
	+DONTMORPH
	+FULLVOLDEATH
	+FLOORCLIP
	-NODROPOFF
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	-COUNTKILL
	MaxStepHeight 96
	Radius 40
	Height 70
	Speed 15
	Health 5600
	Mass 5000
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Tank/Sight"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Tank/Active"
	PainSound "L4D/Tank/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Tank/Death"
	MeleeRange 100
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.2
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
	Obituary "%o underestimated the Tank's throwing abilities."
	HitObituary "%o felt the unpleasant experience of being hulk smashed by the Tank."
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		N029 A 0
		N029 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
	Idle:
		N029 A 2 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N029 B 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Step",6,0.4)
		N029 BB 3 A_Chase
		N029 B 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Step",6,0.4)
		N029 CCDDEE 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Smash")
		N029 O 0 A_FaceTarget
		N029 O 0 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"MeleeClose")
		N029 U 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 UV 5 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",50,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",100,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 WX 5 A_Chase("","")
		Goto See
	MeleeClose:
		N029 O 0 A_Stop
		N029 O 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 OPQR 3 A_FaceTarget
		N029 S 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,250),"L4D/Tank/Punch","")
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,25,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,-25,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 ST 3 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Smash:
		N029 O 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 FGH 4 A_FaceTarget
		N029 IJKL 3 A_FaceTarget
		N029 M 8 A_SpawnItemEx("DogShockwave",50,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 N 5
		Goto See
	Missile:
	RockThrow:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"Melee")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		NA29 A 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 B 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 C 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 D 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",10,0,20,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Pickup",6)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockBit",random(10,-10),random(10,-10),3,frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,1.0),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockBit",random(10,-10),random(10,-10),3,frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,1.0),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 E 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,50,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 F 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,65,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 G 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,80,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 H 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,80,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Throw",5)
		NA29 J 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 K 4 A_CustomMissile("L4DTankRockTrown",40,0,0)
		NA29 L 5
		//TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"EndRockThrow")
		//TNT1 A 0 A_MonsterRefire(0,"EndRockThrow")
		Goto EndRockThrow
	EndRockThrow:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N029 A 2
		N029 A 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DTankScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		NB29 A 0 A_Scream
		NB29 ABCD 6
		NB29 E 35
		NB29 FG 7
		NB29 H 0 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		NB29 H -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DTankScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 1 
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DTankScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor TankSlapDistance
{
	Projectile
	+NOINTERACTION
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+FOILINVUL
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(40,256,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_RadiusThrust(256,256,RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE)
		TNT1 A 1 A_RadiusThrust(512,256,RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_RadiusThrust(2048,256,RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE)
		Stop
	}
}


ACtor TankRockDummy
{
	+NOINTERACTION
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		X142 A 5
		Stop
	}
}


Actor L4DTankRockTrown
{
	Projectile
	Speed 37
	Radius 10
	Height 16
	Damage 50
	DeathSound "L4D/Tank/RockHit"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/RockLoop",7,0.5,1,4)
		X142 AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFFGGGHHHIIIJJJKKKLLLMMMNNNOOOPPP 1 A_Explode(50,40,0,0,40)
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockBit",random(10,-10),random(10,-10),0,frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,0),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

Actor L4DCommonHP : HealthBonus
{
	Inventory.MaxAmount 30
	Inventory.Amount 1
}


Actor L4DCommonSpawner : RandomSpawner
{
	DropItem "L4DCommonMale1"
	DropItem "L4DCommonMale2"
	DropItem "L4DCommonFemale1"
	DropItem "L4DCommonFemale2"
}
Actor L4DCommonMale1
{
	TeleFogSourceType "NewFogSimpler"
	TeleFogDestType "NewFogSimpler"
	var int user_timer;
	var int user_spawncheck;
	var int user_x[2];
	var int user_y[2];
	var int user_nightmare;
	Monster
	Health 30
	Radius 16
	Height 56
	Mass 120
	Speed 12
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Common/Male/Sight"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Common/Male/Active"
	Scale 0.4
	+DONTCORPSE
	+THRUSPECIES
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	-COUNTKILL
	+AMBUSH
	+LOOKALLAROUND
	+ALWAYSTELEFRAG
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	+PUSHABLE
	+DOHARMSPECIES
	PushFactor 0.1
	MaxStepHeight 96
	Species "CommonInfected"
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
	GibHealth 100
//Flesh
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 2.0
	DamageFactor "ZombieRipper", 1.0
	PainChance "Charm", 255
	PainChance "Terror", 255
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 160
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o couldn't keep the infected off of %g self."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N041 A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("L4DZombieHealthSetter",1)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",0)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",0,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",0,y)
	Idle:
		N041 A 10 A_Look
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",user_timer+10)
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_timer>=2100,"Immadie")
		Loop
	Immadie:
		TNT1 A 1 A_Die("NoCount")
		Wait
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_nightmare==1,"Chasing")
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("NightmareToken",1,2,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		N041 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonHP",10)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_nightmare",1)
	Chasing:
		N041 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_spawncheck==1,"See")
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",1,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",1,y)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_x[0]==user_x[1]&&user_y[0]==user_y[1],"Immadie")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_spawncheck",1)
		Loop

	Melee:
		N041 FG 4 A_FaceTarget
		N041 H 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N041 IJ 4 A_FaceTarget
		N041 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N041 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		N041 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N041 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
		N041 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("THRUACTORS",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_DropItem("DMSoulFragment",1,1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
	Death.NoCount: //Don't drop souls if it doesn't count.
		N041 L 0 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N041 LMNOPQRST 4
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,1,2,3,4,5,6)
		N041 UUUUUUUUUU 35
		N041 U 2 A_FadeOut(0.08)
		Wait
	XDeath:
		"####" "#" 0 A_DropItem("DMSoulFragment",1,1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM,0,GibTID)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 0 A_DropItem("DMSoulFragment",1,1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GenericFreezeDeath 
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		//"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks // [Ms] Makes 28 shards -- blasphemously many!
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("misc/icebreak")
		"####" "#####" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AEIceChunk",random(-12,12),random(-12,12),random(6,48),random(-2,2),random(-2,2),random(-2,2),0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION) // 5 ought to be 'nuff
		Stop
	}
}

Actor L4DCommonMale2 : L4DCommonMale1 
{
	// [Ms] All properties are identical.
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		N042 A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("L4DZombieHealthSetter",1)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",0)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",0,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",0,y)
	Idle:
		N042 A 10 A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",user_timer+10)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_timer>=2100,"Immadie")
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_nightmare==1,"Chasing")
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("NightmareToken",1,2,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		N041 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonHP",10)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_nightmare",1)
	Chasing:
		N042 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_spawncheck==1,"See")
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",1,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",1,y)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_x[0]==user_x[1]&&user_y[0]==user_y[1],"Immadie")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_spawncheck",1)
		Loop
	Melee:
		N042 FG 4 A_FaceTarget
		N042 H 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N042 IJ 4 A_FaceTarget
		N042 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N042 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_DropItem("DMSoulFragment",1,1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
	Death.NoCount:
		N042 L 4 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N042 MNOPQ 4
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,1,2,3,4,5,6)
		N042 RRRRRRRRRR 35
		N042 R 2 A_FadeOut(0.08)
		Wait

		// Immadie, XDeath, Disint and Ice are identical.
	}
}

{

	States
	{

Actor L4DCommonFemale2 : L4DCommonFemale1
{
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		N046 A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("L4DZombieHealthSetter",1)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",0)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",0,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",0,y)
	Idle:
		N046 A 10 A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_timer",user_timer+10)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_timer>=2100,"Immadie")
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_nightmare==1,"Chasing")
		N041 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("NightmareToken",1,2,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		N041 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonHP",10)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_nightmare",1)
	Chasing:
		N046 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_spawncheck==1,"See")
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_x",1,x)
		N041 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_y",1,y)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_x[0]==user_x[1]&&user_y[0]==user_y[1],"Immadie")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_spawncheck",1)
		Loop
	Melee:
		N046 FG 4 A_FaceTarget
		N046 H 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N046 IJ 4 A_FaceTarget
		N046 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,2),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N046 A 8
		Goto See
	}
}

    }

Actor L4DBoomer
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment" 64
	var int user_skill;
	var int user_angle;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 450
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 10
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Boomer/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Boomer/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Boomer/Explo"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Boomer/Idle"
	MeleeRange 50
	MaxTargetRange 1024
	Scale 0.8
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	MaxStepHeight 96
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
	Obituary "%o was biled by the Boomer."
	HitObituary "The boomer was too fat for %o to handle."
	States
	{
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N028 A 0
		N028 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
	Idle:
		N028 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N028 B 3 A_Chase 	N028 B 2 A_Chase
		N028 C 3 A_Chase 	N028 C 2 A_Chase
		N028 D 3 A_Chase 	N028 D 2 A_Chase
		N028 E 3 A_Chase 	N028 E 2 A_Chase
		Loop
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Melee2")
		N028 JK 3 A_FaceTarget
		N028 L 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Melee2:
		N028 MN 3 A_FaceTarget
		N028 O 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Boomer/Vomit")
		N028 FFFFFFFFGH 4 A_FaceTarget
		N028 I 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPuke",35,0,0)
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N028 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DBoomerScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(128,128,XF_NOTMISSILE,0,64)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",0)
	Looper:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_angle>=360,"EndLoop")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeInvisible",40,0,user_angle)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",user_angle+5)
		Loop
	EndLoop:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PBExplosionDebrisless",0,0,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	PukeFromExplo:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("PukeObscureVision",1)
		Goto Death+3
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DBoomerScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}
Actor BoomerPuke 
{
	Projectile
	-NOGRAVITY
	Gravity 0.05
	Radius 5
	Height 10
	Speed 30
	Scale 0.5
	Damage 0
	RenderStyle Add
	Alpha 0.8
	Translation "0:255=%[0,0,0]:[0.55,0.63,0.125]" 
	PoisonDamage 20
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+DONTSPLASH
	+SeekerMissile
	DamageType Chaos
	+FORCEPAIN
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_seekerMissile(0,0)
		X022 AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 A_SpawnItemEx("PukeDrop",0,random(3,-3),random(0,6),0.01,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		Goto Spawn+2
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("halflife/monsters/bullsquid/spitehit")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfTracerCloser(32,"BlurVision")
		TNT1 A 10
		Stop
	BlurVision:
		TNT1 A 10 A_GiveInventory("PukeObscureVision",1,AAPTR_TRACER)
		Stop
	}
}

	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,random(4,10),0,1)
		VOM2 ABCDEF 4 Bright
		Goto Spawn+2
	Death:
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BSSpitExtra",0,0,4,random(1,-1),random(1,-1),random(0,2),0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		VOM2 A 1 A_FadeOut
		Wait
	}
}

Actor L4DJockey
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment" 64
	var int user_skill;
	var int user_countermain;
	var int user_countersecondary;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 350
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 200
	Speed 11
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Jockey/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Jockey/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Jockey/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Jockey/Active"
	Scale 0.5
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+FOILINVUL
	MaxStepHeight 96
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "A Jockey rode %o so hard, %o was put away dead."
	HitObituary "%o tripped over a Jockey."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N040 A 0
		N040 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
	Idle:
		N040 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N040 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		N040 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("","")
		Goto See
		
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		N040 G 3 A_FaceTarget
		N040 G 0 A_Recoil(-28)
		N040 H 1 ThrustThingZ(0,35,0,0)
	LeapLoop:
		N040 I 0 A_CheckFloor("LeapEnd")
		N040 I 1 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"Ride")
		Loop
	LeapEnd:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("fiend/land")
		N040 J 4 A_Stop
		N040 K 4
		Goto See  
		
	Ride:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Jockey/Rape",6,1,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countermain",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",0)
	MoveDistortion:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(1)
		N040 F 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"EndRide",AAPTR_TARGET)
		N040 F 0 A_JumpIf(IsPointerEqual(AAPTR_TARGET,AAPTR_NULL),"EndRide")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFlag("DONTTHRUST",3,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Unrideable",1,2,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("JockeyRideHack",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",0)
	RideLoop:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_countersecondary>=5,"MoveDistortion")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_countermain>=350,"EndRide")
		N040 F 1 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,-10,0,48,180,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFlag("DONTTHRUST",3,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Unrideable",1,2,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("JockeyRideHack2",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countermain",user_countermain+random(0,2))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",user_countersecondary+1)
		Loop
	EndRide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
		
	Pain:
		N040 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DJockeyScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		N040 L 0 A_StopSound(6)
		N040 L 0 A_Scream
		N040 L 4 A_Fall
		N040 MNOP 4
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,1,2,3,4,5,6)
		N040 QQQQQQQQQQ 35
		N040 Q 2 A_FadeOut(0.08)
		Wait
	XDeath:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DJockeyScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DJockeyScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DJockeyScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}

{ Inventory.MaxAmount 1 }

	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	States
	{

		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(random(15,-15),random(15,-15),0,1)
		Stop
	}
}

	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	States
	{

		TNT1 A 0 A_SetAngle(angle+random(5,-5))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetPitch(pitch+random(1,-1))
		Stop
	}

//======================================================================================
//======================================================================================
Actor L4DHunter
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment" 64
	var int user_skill;
	var int user_type;
	var int user_timer;
	var int user_count;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 450
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 150
	Speed 10
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Hunter/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Hunter/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Hunter/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Hunter/Stalk"
	Scale 0.35
	MeleeRange 80
	MaxTargetRange 512
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	MaxStepHeight 96
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o failed to dodge a Hunter."
	HitObituary "%o was pounced by a Hunter."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N039 A 0
		N039 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
	Idle:
		N039 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 
		{
			A_RearrangePointers(DefPtr, DefPtr, NullPtr, 4);
			// Don't leap at enemies that are blocked by solid non-damageable entities.
			if (A_CheckLOF("Null",CLOFF_SETTRACER|CLOFF_SKIPOBSTACLES|CLOFF_SKIPTARGET|CLOFF_JUMPOBJECT|CLOFF_MUSTBESOLID))
			{	A_Chase("Melee","");	}
			else
			{	A_Chase;	}
			
			A_SetUserVar(user_timer,0);
			A_SetUserVar(user_count,0);
		}
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		N039 B 0 
		{
			A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1);
			A_SetUserVar(user_timer,0);
			A_SetUserVar(user_count,0);
		}
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",0)
		Goto See
		
	Melee:
		N039 FG 3 A_FaceTarget
		N039 H 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(5,10),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N039 IJ 3 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
		
	Missile:
		N039 K 3
		{
			A_SetUserVar(user_timer,0);
			A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1);
			A_PlaySound("L4D/Hunter/Lunge",6);
			A_FaceTarget;
			A_RearrangePointers(DefPtr, DefPtr, NullPtr, 4);
		}
		N039 L 1 
		{
			if (A_JumpIfHigherOrLower("Null","")) //Target is below
			{
				A_FaceTarget(0,0,0,0,FAF_TOP,-4);
			}
			else if (A_JumpIfHigherOrLower("","Null")) //Target is above
			{
				A_FaceTarget(0,0,0,0,FAF_TOP,10 + GetDistance(true)/5.0);
			}
			else //Target's on (near) equal z
			{
				A_FaceTarget(0,0,0,0,FAF_TOP,GetDistance(true)/5.0);
			}
			A_ChangeVelocity(cos(-pitch)*40,0,sin(pitch)*40,CVF_RELATIVE|CVF_REPLACE);
			//A_Recoil(-38);
			//ThrustThingZ(0,35,0,0);
		}
		N039 LL 1
	LeapLoop:
		N039 M 1
		{
			A_RearrangePointers(DefPtr, DefPtr, NullPtr, 4);
			A_SpawnItemEx("L4DHunterTrail",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE);
			if (A_CheckFloor("Null"))
			{	return state("LeapEnd");	}
			if (velz == 0)
			{
				A_SetUserVar(user_timer, user_timer + 1);
				if (user_timer >= 35)
				{	return state("LeapEnd");	}
			}
			if (A_CheckLOF("Null",CLOFF_SETTRACER|CLOFF_JUMPENEMY|CLOFF_JUMPNONHOSTILE|CLOFF_JUMPFRIEND|CLOFF_JUMPOBJECT|CLOFF_FROMBASE|CLOFF_MUSTBESHOOTABLE,64+radius,0,0,0,height/2.0) ||
				A_CheckLOF("Null",CLOFF_SETTRACER|CLOFF_JUMPENEMY|CLOFF_JUMPNONHOSTILE|CLOFF_JUMPFRIEND|CLOFF_JUMPOBJECT|CLOFF_FROMBASE|CLOFF_MUSTBESHOOTABLE|CLOFF_ALLOWNULL|CLOFF_JUMP_ON_MISS,64+radius,0,0,-pitch,height/2.0,0,NullPtr))
			{	
				if (IsPointerEqual(Tracer,NullPtr) || !A_CheckFlag(SHOOTABLE,"Null",Tracer))
				{	return state("LeapEnd");	}
				return state("QuickMelee");	
			}
			return state(0);
		}
		Loop
	LeapEnd:
		N039 N 4 
		{
			A_PlaySound("fiend/land");
			A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0);
			A_Stop;
		}
		N039 O 4
	LeapLander:
		"####" "#" 1 A_JumpIf(velz >= 0 || z <= GetZAt(0,0) || z <= floorz,"LeepEndCont")
		Loop
	LeepEndCont:
		"----" A 0 //Don't bother leaping again if something else is in the way such as a static actor.
		{
			if (A_CheckLOF("Null",CLOFF_SKIPENEMY|CLOFF_SKIPFRIEND|CLOFF_SKIPNONHOSTILE|CLOFF_SKIPTARGET|CLOFF_JUMPOBJECT|CLOFF_SETTRACER|CLOFF_MUSTBESOLID))
			{	return state("SeeNoMissile");	}
			if (user_count < 6)
			{
				A_SetUserVar(user_count, user_count + randompick(1,1,2,2,2,3,3));
			}
			else
			{
				A_SetUserVar(user_count, 0);
				return state("SeeNoMissile");
			}
			return state("Missile");
		}
	QuickMelee:
		"####" "#" 1 
		{
			A_DamageTracer(random(75,150),"Melee",DMSS_AFFECTARMOR);
			A_PlaySound("quake4/Misc/MeleeHit",5);
			//A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(75,150),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1);
			A_PlaySound("fiend/land");
			A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0);	
		}
		N039 N 4 A_Stop
		N039 O 4
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	Pain:
		N039 A 8 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DHunterScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		N039 P 2 A_Fall
		N039 QRSTUVWXY 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,1,2,3,4,5,6)
		N039 ZZZZZZZZZZ 35
		N039 Z 2 A_FadeOut(0.08)
		Wait
	XDeath:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DHunterScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DHunterScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}

Actor L4DWitchWander
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment"
	var int user_skill;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 2500
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 8
	PainChance 256
	SeeSound ""
	DeathSound "L4D/Witch/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Witch/Growl"
	Scale 0.47
	MeleeRange 80
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	MaxStepHeight 96
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 0
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 0
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 0
	Obituary "%o played with fire by startling a witch."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		NB30 A 0
		NB30 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CryWander",6)//this one will play always the 1st time.
	Idle:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CryWander",random(5,7))
		NB30 A 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		NB30 B 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		NB30 C 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		NB30 D 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
	Alert:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CryWander",random(5,7))
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(80,"Chase")
		NB30 A 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander 	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(80,"Chase")
		NB30 B 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(80,"Chase")
		NB30 C 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(80,"Chase")
		NB30 D 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Wander	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(80,"Chase")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE) 	//this is because if player dies while the witch is in this state, it will still try to attack the corpse
		Loop			//but using A_Chase is an internal check where if player is dead, it returns to "Spawn" or "Idle"
	Chase:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/Sight",6)
		N030 AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Chase
		Goto Chase+1
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 E 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 F 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 G 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,300),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 H 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Recoil(-4)
		Goto Chase+1
	Pain:
		N030 A 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		Goto Chase
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	XDeath:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCommonScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}
Actor L4DWitchSitting
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment"
	var int user_skill;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1	
	Health 2500
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 8
	PainChance 256
	SeeSound ""
	DeathSound "L4D/Witch/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Witch/Anger"
	Scale 0.47
	MeleeRange 80
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	MaxStepHeight 96
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 0
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 0
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 0
	Obituary "%o played with fire by startling a witch."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		NB30 A 0
		NB30 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SkillCountSetter",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",6)//this one will play always the 1st time.
	Idle:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 ABCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"NoHeadQuickBob")	//chance to skip the headbobbing
		NA30 EDCBCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look				//performs full cycle headbob
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"NoHeadQuickBob")	//chooses to exit the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)				//or chooses to play the sound and loop the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		Goto Idle+7
		
	NoHeadQuickBob:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 DCBA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		Goto Idle
	// This whole part is the exact same as above, except that instead of A_Look is using A_JumpIfCloser
	See:
	Active:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 ABCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(128,"Chase")
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"NoHeadQuickBobActive")	//chance to skip the headbobbing
		NA30 EDCBCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(128,"Chase")				//performs full cycle headbob
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"NoHeadQuickBobActive")	//chooses to exit the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(220,2)				//or chooses to play the sound and loop the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		Goto Active+6
	NoHeadQuickBobActive:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(128,"Chase")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 DCBA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(128,"Chase")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(128,"Chase")
		Goto Active

	Chase:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/Sight",CHAN_VOICE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		N030 AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Chase
		Goto Chase+2
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 E 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 F 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 G 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,300),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 H 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Recoil(-4)
		Goto Chase+2
	Pain:
		N030 A 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		Goto Chase
	Death:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),velx,vely,velz,random(140,220),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_ABSOLUTEMOMENTUM)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DWitchScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}

Actor L4DCharger
{
	DropItem "DMSoulFragment" 64
	var int user_skill;
	var int user_count;
	var int user_angle;
	var int user_x;
	var int user_y;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 500
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 20
	PainChance 24
	SeeSound "L4D/Charger/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Charger/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Charger/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Charger/Active"
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DROPOFF
	+NOBLOCKMONST
	+DONTMORPH
	-COUNTKILL
	MaxStepHeight 96
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o was pounded into Wall Pancake(TM) by the charger."
	HitObituary "%o failed to realize the Charger's good arm is as strong as a Tank's."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N031 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase("Melee","")
		Goto See
	Melee:
		N031 J 4 A_FaceTarget
		N031 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(10,60),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N031 L 4 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Charger/Charge",6)
		N031 AAA 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		N048 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChargerHitboxSensor",20,0,20,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_SETTARGET)
		N048 M 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",angle)
	Charge:
		N031 FF 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
		N031 GG 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
		N031 HH 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
		N031 II 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
		N048 M 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		N048 M 0 A_JumpIf(user_count>=12,"EndCharge")
		Loop
	Pain.Rammer:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 HealThing(2)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1000,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	EndCharge:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 A_GiveInventory("DogHitSomething",1)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	Pain.Canceller:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 HealThing(2)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1000,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	Pain:
		"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		"####" "#" 8 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DChargerScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 5 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DChargerScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DChargerScore",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	}
}

Actor AEL4DTank 		//cyberdemon
{
	DropItem "MegaHeart" 128
	DropItem "HalfWeaponPower" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner"
	Monster
	RipLevelMin 1
	+BOSS
	+BOSSDEATH
	+NOICEDEATH
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+DONTBLAST
	+DONTMORPH
	+FULLVOLDEATH
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DONTCORPSE
	Radius 40
	Height 70
	Speed 15
	Health 6500
	Mass 5000
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Tank/Sight"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Tank/Active"
	PainSound "L4D/Tank/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Tank/Death"
	MeleeRange 100
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 0
	PainChance "Terror", 0
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Drain", 40
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
	DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
	Obituary "%o was flattened by the Tank's rocks."
	HitObituary "%o was unfortunate enough to be hulk smashed by a Tank."
	States
	{	
	Spawn:
		N029 A 2 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N029 B 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Step",6,0.4)
		N029 BB 3 A_Chase
		N029 B 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Step",6,0.4)
		N029 CCDDEE 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Smash")
		N029 O 0 A_FaceTarget
		N029 O 0 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"MeleeClose")
		N029 U 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 UV 5 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",50,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 W 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",100,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 WX 5 A_Chase("","")
		Goto See
	MeleeClose:
		N029 O 0 A_Stop
		N029 O 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 OPQR 3 A_FaceTarget
		N029 S 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,250),"L4D/Tank/Punch","")
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,25,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankSlapDistance",75,0,0,0,0,0,-25,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 ST 3 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Smash:
		N029 O 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Tank/Attack",5,1,0)
		N029 FGH 4 A_FaceTarget
		N029 IJKL 3 A_FaceTarget
		N029 M 8 A_SpawnItemEx("DogShockwave",50,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N029 N 5
		Goto See
	Missile:
	RockThrow:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"Melee")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		NA29 A 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 B 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 C 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 D 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",10,0,20,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockBit",random(10,-10),random(10,-10),3,frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,1.0),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockBit",random(10,-10),random(10,-10),3,frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,-6.0),frandom(6.0,1.0),random(0,359),SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 E 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,50,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 F 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,65,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 G 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,80,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 H 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,70,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 I 4 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TankRockDummy",1,0,80,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		NA29 J 4 A_FaceTarget
		NA29 K 4 A_CustomMissile("L4DTankRockTrown",40,0,0)
		NA29 L 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"EndRockThrow")
		TNT1 A 0 A_MonsterRefire(0,"EndRockThrow")
		Loop
	EndRockThrow:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N029 A 2
		N029 A 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		NB29 A 0 A_Scream
		NB29 ABCD 6
		NB29 E 35
		NB29 FG 7
		NB29 H 0 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		NB29 H -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,60),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,60),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,60),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)

		Stop

	Death.PlasmaDisint:

	PainChance "Terror", 255

		Loop
	See:

		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Loop

		N041 FG 4 A_FaceTarget
		N041 H 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(10,20),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)

		N041 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(10,20),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N041 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		N041 L 4 A_Fall
		N041 MNOPQRST 4
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N041 U -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop

		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeath+1
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:

Actor AEL4DSmoker		//baron of hell
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 210
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 1000
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 600
	Speed 10
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Smoker/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Smoker/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Smoker/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Smoker/Sight"
	MeleeRange 70
	MaxTargetRange 1024
	Scale 0.41
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	+DONTCORPSE
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
	DamageFactor "PoisonCloud", 0.0
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255		//pretty much useless, since the bugs will die because of the poison
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o was strangulated by a smoker."
	HitObituary "%o should never have attempted to befriend a smoker."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)			Goto See 
	
	Spawn:
		N043 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N043 B 3 A_Chase 	N043 B 2 A_Chase
		N043 C 3 A_Chase 	N043 C 2 A_Chase
		N043 D 3 A_Chase 	N043 D 2 A_Chase
		N043 E 3 A_Chase 	N043 E 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Loop
	DefileDecide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(8,1)
		Goto See
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		Wait
	Melee:
		N043 FG 3 A_FaceTarget
		N043 H 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N043 I 3
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,"SmokeTrap")
	Tongue:
		N043 N 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Smoker/Warning")
		N043 JJJJJJK 4 A_FaceTarget
		N043 L 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokerTongue",35,0,0)
		N043 LLLLLLLLLLLLLMMMMMM 1 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"InstaMelee")
		Goto See
	SmokeTrap:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Tongue")
		N043 N 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Smoker/Sight")
		N043 JJJJJJK 4 A_FaceTarget
		N043 L 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokerTrap",0,0,0)
		N043 LMM 4
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Tongue")
		Goto See
	InstaMelee:
		N043 G 0 A_FaceTarget
		N043 G 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N043 H 3
		N043 I 3	
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N043 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokerTrap",0,0,0)
		N043 N 3 A_Scream
		N043 O 3 A_Fall
		N043 PQ 3
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N043 R -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	DefileDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeath+1
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SmokerTrap",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor AEL4DBoomer		//fatso
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 210
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	var int user_angle;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 600
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 10
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Boomer/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Boomer/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Boomer/Explo"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Boomer/Idle"
	MeleeRange 50
	MaxTargetRange 1024
	Scale 0.8
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 96
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o was biled by a boomer."
	HitObituary "%o couldn't handle the boomer's crushing fat."
	States
	{
	Pain.Chaos:
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
		Goto See
	Pain.ChaosExpl1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.ChaosExpl2:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)		Goto See
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)			Goto See 
	
	Spawn:
		N028 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N028 B 3 A_Chase 	N028 B 2 A_Chase
		N028 C 3 A_Chase 	N028 C 2 A_Chase
		N028 D 3 A_Chase 	N028 D 2 A_Chase
		N028 E 3 A_Chase 	N028 E 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Loop
	DefileDecide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(10,1)
		Goto See
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		Wait
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Melee2")
		N028 JK 3 A_FaceTarget
		N028 L 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Melee2:
		N028 MN 3 A_FaceTarget
		N028 O 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,100),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Boomer/Vomit")
		N028 FFFFFFFFGH 4 A_FaceTarget
		N028 I 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPuke",35,0,0)
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		N028 II 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))	N028 I 1 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeFx",35,3,random(5,-5))
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N028 A 8
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(128,128,XF_NOTMISSILE,0,64)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",0)
	Looper:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_angle>=360,"EndLoop")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("BoomerPukeInvisible",60,0,user_angle)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",user_angle+5)
		Loop
	EndLoop:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PBExplosionDebrisless",0,0,35,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	PukeFromExplo:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("PukeObscureVision",1)
		Goto Death+3
	DefileDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Death+1
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}
Actor BoomerPuke2 : BoomerPuke
{
	Damage 25
}

Actor AEL4DJockey		//Hell knight
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 160
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	var int user_countermain;
	var int user_countersecondary;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 400
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 150
	Speed 11
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Jockey/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Jockey/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Jockey/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Jockey/Active"
	Scale 0.5
	+DONTCORPSE
	+FLOORCLIP
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "A Jockey rode %o so hard, he was put away dead."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)			Goto See 
	
	Spawn:
		N040 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N040 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		N040 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("","")
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Goto See
	DefileDecide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(10,1)
		Goto See
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		Wait
		
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		N040 G 3 A_FaceTarget
		N040 G 0 A_Recoil(-28)
		N040 H 1 ThrustThingZ(0,35,0,0)
	LeapLoop:
		N040 I 0 A_CheckFloor("LeapEnd")
		N040 I 1 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"Ride")
		Loop
	LeapEnd:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("fiend/land")
		N040 J 4 A_Stop
		N040 K 4
		Goto See  
		
	Ride:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Jockey/Rape",6,1,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countermain",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",0)
	MoveDistortion:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMeleeAttack(1)
		N040 F 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"EndRide",AAPTR_TARGET)
		N040 F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Unrideable",1,2,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("JockeyRideHack",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",0)
	RideLoop:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_countersecondary>=5,"MoveDistortion")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_countermain>=350,"EndRide")
		N040 F 1 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,-10,0,48,180,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("JockeyRideHack2",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countermain",user_countermain+random(0,2))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_countersecondary",user_countersecondary+1)
		Loop
	EndRide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_StopSound(6)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
		
	Pain:
		N040 A 8 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		N040 L 0 A_StopSound(6)
		N040 L 0 A_Scream
		N040 L 4 A_Fall
		N040 MNOP 4
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N040 Q -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	DefileDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeath+1
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor AEL4DHunter		//archvile
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 900
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 120
	Speed 10
	PainChance 64
	SeeSound "L4D/Hunter/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Hunter/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Hunter/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Hunter/Stalk"
	Scale 0.35
	MeleeRange 80
	MaxTargetRange 512
	+DONTCORPSE
	+STEALTH
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 96
	PainChance "Terror", 96
	PainChance "Drain", 64
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
	Obituary "%o couldn't dodge out of the way of a Hunter."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)			Goto See 
	
	Spawn:
		N039 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N039 BBCCDDEE 2 A_Chase("Melee","")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",0)
		Goto See
		
	Melee:
		N039 FG 3 A_FaceTarget
		N039 H 3 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(20,80),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N039 IJ 3 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
		
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Hunter/Lunge",6)
		N039 K 3 A_FaceTarget
		N039 L 0 A_Recoil(-38)
		N039 L 1 ThrustThingZ(0,35,0,0)
		N039 LL 1
	LeapLoop:
		N039 M 0 A_CheckFloor("LeapEnd")
		N039 M 1 A_JumpIfCloser(64,"QuickMelee")
		Loop
	LeapEnd:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("fiend/land")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		N039 N 4 A_Stop
		N039 O 4
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	QuickMelee:
		"####" "#" 1 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(50,150),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		"####" "#" 0 HealThing(random(20,50))
		Goto LeapEnd
	Pain:
		N039 A 8 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		N039 P 2 A_Fall
		N039 QRSTUVWXY 2
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N039 Z -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor AEL4DWitch		//archvile
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 1000
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 8
	PainChance 256
	SeeSound ""
	DeathSound "L4D/Witch/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Witch/Anger"
	Scale 0.47
	MeleeRange 80
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	+DONTMORPH
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 0
	PainChance "Terror", 96
	PainChance "Drain", 64
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
	Obituary "%o played with fire by startling a Witch."
	States
	{
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	Pain.Defile:		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)			Goto See 
	
	Spawn:
		NB30 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",6)//this one will play always the 1st time.
	Idle:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 ABCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"NoHeadQuickBob")	//chance to skip the headbobbing
		NA30 EDCBCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look				//performs full cycle headbob
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"NoHeadQuickBob")	//chooses to exit the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)				//or chooses to play the sound and loop the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		Goto Idle+7
		
	NoHeadQuickBob:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 DCBA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Look
		Goto Idle
	// This whole part is the exact same as above, except that instead of A_Look is using A_JumpIfCloser
	See:
	Active:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 ABCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Chase")
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"NoHeadQuickBobActive")	//chance to skip the headbobbing
		NA30 EDCBCD 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Chase")				//performs full cycle headbob
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"NoHeadQuickBobActive")	//chooses to exit the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(220,2)				//or chooses to play the sound and loop the headbobbing
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		Goto Active+6
	NoHeadQuickBobActive:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 EEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Chase")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(210,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/CrySit",random(5,7))
		NA30 DCBA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Chase")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9)
		NA30 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 8 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_JumpIfCloser(256,"Chase")
		Goto Active

	Chase:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Witch/Sight",CHAN_VOICE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		N030 AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Chase
		Goto Chase+2
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 E 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 F 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_FaceTarget	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 G 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(30,70),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(-4)
		N030 H 4 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_Recoil(-4)
		Goto Chase+2
	Pain:
		N030 A 1 Light("L4DWitchLight") A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		Goto Chase
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor AEL4DCharger		//hell knight
{
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "RandomWeaponPower" 190
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	var int user_count;
	var int user_angle;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Health 500
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 20
	PainChance 24
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "L4D/Charger/Sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Charger/Pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Charger/Death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Charger/Active"
	DamageFactor "SpitterAcid", 0.1
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	
	PainChance "Charm", 192
	PainChance "Terror", 192
	PainChance "Defile", 255
	PainChance "Drain", 110
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
	Obituary "%o was pounded into Wall Pancake(TM) by the Charger."
	HitObituary "%o should've realized the Charger's good arm is as strong as a Tank's."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		N031 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Loop
	SeeNoMissile:
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase("Melee","")
		N031 BCDE 4 A_Chase("Melee","")
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDecide")
		Goto See
	DefileDecide:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(10,1)
		Goto See
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		Wait
	Melee:
		N031 J 4 A_FaceTarget
		N031 K 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(10,60),"quake4/Misc/MeleeHit","quake4/Misc/Swing","Normal",1)
		N031 L 4 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("L4D/Charger/Charge",6)
		N031 AAA 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		N048 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChargerHitboxSensor",20,0,20,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_SETTARGET)
		//N048 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogHitboxSensor",30,0,10,0,0,0,90,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		//N048 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogHitboxSensor",30,0,10,0,0,0,180,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		//N048 K 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogHitboxSensor",30,0,10,0,0,0,270,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N048 M 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle",angle)
	Charge:
		N031 FF 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetAngle(user_angle)
		N031 GG 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetAngle(user_angle)
		N031 HH 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetAngle(user_angle)
		N031 II 1 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetAngle(user_angle)
		N048 M 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		N048 M 0 A_JumpIf(user_count>=12,"EndCharge")
		Loop
	Pain.Rammer:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 HealThing(2)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1000,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	EndCharge:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 A_GiveInventory("DogHitSomething",1)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	Pain.Canceller:
		N031 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		N031 A 2 HealThing(1)
		N031 A 0 A_TakeInventory("DogHitSomething",1000,0)
		Goto SeeNoMissile
	Pain:
		
		"####" "#" 1 A_Pain
		"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		"####" "#" 7
		//"####" "#" 0 A_TakeInventory("IDied",100)
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"DefileDeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 5 A_Fall
		Stop
	DefileDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Death+1
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}
}

Actor ChargerHitboxSensor
{
	var int user_angle[5];
	Projectile
	+DONTREFLECT
	+FOILINVUL
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	RenderStyle None
	Alpha 0.75
	Radius 30
	Height 20
	Speed 10
	Damage 1
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
	Waiting:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"End",AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,"End",AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("DogHitSomething",1,"End",AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(2,128,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetAngle(angle+random(5,25))
		TNT1 A 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,20,0,10,0,WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE,"Waiting")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"End",AAPTR_TARGET)
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_DamageTarget(1,"Rammer",DMSS_NOFACTOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DogHitSomething",1,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogHitsWall",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogShockwave",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS)
		Stop
	Crash:
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DogHitSomething",1,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DogHitsActor",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(random(100,400),128,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_RadiusThrust(2248,512,RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_DamageTarget(1,"Rammer",DMSS_NOFACTOR)
		Stop
	End:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DogHitSomething",1,AAPTR_TARGET)
		TNT1 A 0 A_DamageTarget(1,"Rammer",DMSS_NOFACTOR)
		Stop
	}
}
