Actor AEL4DRochelle		//baron
{
	DropItem "AEoDChainsawItem" 32
	DropItem "HealthBottle" 64
	DropItem "HealthBottle" 64
	DropItem "CellBigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "CellBigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
	var int user_targetcheck;
	Monster	RipLevelMin 1
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 450
	Speed 15
	Health 1000
	Painchance 20
	SeeSound "L4D/Rochelle/sight"
	PainSound "L4D/Rochelle/pain"
	DeathSound "L4D/Rochelle/death"
	ActiveSound "L4D/Rochelle/idle"
	Scale 0.34
	MeleeRange 100
	+DONTCORPSE
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	PainChance "Charm", 96
	PainChance "Terror", 96
	PainChance "Drain", 64
	PainChance "Defile", 0
	PainChance "Chaos", 255
	PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
	PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
	Obituary "Rochelle got ugly with %o."
	States
	{
	Pain.Charm:			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)				Goto See
	Pain.Terror:		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)			Goto See
	Pain.Drain:			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)	Goto Pain
	
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawidl2",6,1,15)
	Idle:
		N037 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_targetcheck",0)
		N037 A 10 A_Look
		Wait
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_targetcheck==1,"SeeReady")
		N037 BB 2 A_Chase("","")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("MeleeEnable",0)
		N037 CC 2 A_Chase("","")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("MeleeEnable",0)
		N037 DD 2 A_Chase("","")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("MeleeEnable",0)
		N037 EE 2 A_Chase("","")
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInLOS("MeleeEnable",0)
		Loop
	MeleeEnable:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_targetcheck",1)
	SeeReady:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawidl2",6,1,15)
		TNT1 A 0 //A_PrintBold("Normal")
		N037 B 2 A_Chase("","")			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 B 2 A_Chase("","Missile")	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 C 2 A_Chase("","")			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 C 2 A_Chase("","Missile")	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 D 2 A_Chase("","")			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 D 2 A_Chase("","Missile")	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 E 2 A_Chase("","")			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 E 2 A_Chase("","Missile")	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(50,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		Goto See+2
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_PrintBold("Crazy")
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(4,0,0,1)
		N037 B 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 B 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 B 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		N037 C 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 C 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 C 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(4,0,0,1)
		N037 D 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 D 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 D 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(5,0,0,1)
		N037 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		N037 E 1 A_JumpIfCloser(60,"Melee")	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RochelleCsawDummy",0,0,35,50,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(32,"See")
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sawful2",6,1,15)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		N037 F 2 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,random(7,16),"RochelleCSawPuff",110,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		N037 F 2 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,random(7,16),"RochelleCSawPuffNopain",110,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget(0,0)
		N037 F 2 A_CustomBulletAttack(0,0,1,random(7,16),"RochelleCSawPuffNopain",110,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Chase("","",CHF_DONTMOVE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(100,"Melee")
		Goto See
	Pain:
		N037 A 7 A_Pain
		N037 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_targetcheck",1)
		Goto See
	Death:
		N037 G 0 A_StopSound(6)
		N037 G 3 A_Scream
		N037 H 3 A_Fall
		N037 IJK 3
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		N037 L -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Death.UnholyDisint:
	Death.PlasmaDisint:
	Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
	}

The above do not house interhub carrying capabilities because it's only recorded
on a per-map basis. The below, however, do carry over. This is basically for the
junkies that love keeping score and stats of all the things they kill.
*/

	Inventory.InterHubAmount 35000

Actor L4DScoreOrganizer : CustomInventory
{
	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	+INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
	Inventory.MaxAmount 0
	States
	{
	Use:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("L4DCurrentTotal",30001,"Reorganize1",AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		Stop
	Reorganize1:
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("L4DCurrentTotal",30001,0,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCCMultiplier",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("L4DCurrentTotal",1,AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		Stop
	}
}
